118294658290109853583</userid>
<Name>Angel Calderon< /Name><time>1607473650331<//time><rate>1</rate>< Review>
Overpriced, bland, nothing like the pictures on their IG account, no longer serving sushi, and hours are off. Their busiest days are on taco Tuesdays, that says a lot about this place. You have to have an instagram account to check out their menu. Not even that, you have to have service on your phone to check their menu. The tacos aren't even 1 dollar, only the "street tacos" are a dollar...on taco tuesday. The taquero couldn't be bothered to serve the plate with one of each, we were told one plate had to have 3 tacos with only one type of meat. Basically the taquero didn't want to work that day. I missed the chance of going when it opened about a year ago, I'm pretty sure it would have been a totally different experience since everyone in Salinas were hyping this place up. At the end of the service, the guy in charge was pretty much asking for a tip... reminded me of Chinese restaurants. We ended up at about 100 dollars for 16 tacos! The drinks are basic and overpriced. The only magical part about the food was the fried tortilla and the added cheese (this is what made it expensive). The birria is whatever, there are hole in the wall places in Salinas that do a good job with cooking birria, and they actually use goat meat! There are plenty of other good taquerias in Salinas..I mean it is Salinas after all. So much for trying to support local businesses.<//Review>

< review>
My first time here. The food was pretty creative and good---my friend and I ordered baja tacos, poke tacos, a Korean bbq taco, and a jalapeno roll. We agreed everything was tasty, albeit the tuna in the poke tacos had a slight fishy taste. Here's the thing---be prepared for a mashup of flavors. The menu was unexpected---an aguachile sushi roll (rojo o verde), a Hot Cheetos roll, and the poke taco came in a hard taco shell. It was busy while we were there---and we concluded it's a good place for drinks, and getting a bite to eat...in that order. That being said, they get 4 stars for the understaffing. Our server was handling the whole place herself. Not her fault, but when it gets busy, add the loud jukebox, it's hard to flag down a server for the check. Not to worry, though...we'll be back.</review>

<user>102136718024625025379</user><text>The people at the facility are pleasant and thorough. The surgery was quick and professional. Beware the upsell. Make sure you ask about all options as they will pitch only the most expensive. Ask questions. My cataract surgery went well. I can see better at night and see the difference between black and blue again. What they didn't tell me was that my macular degeneration would continue to impede my vision so did I need the super expensive lenses?, likely not. My bad for not asking I guess, but I feel it's something they should have told me. I could have saved thousands with that information.
The experience was fine, but be prepared to miss at least 3 days of work and time off for pre-surgery physical and multiple eye appts before and after. The procedure was quick but there is so much more than that. Just ask lots of questions and make an informed decision even if that means delaying surgery until you grasp everything that's involved. Regrets? A few. I was too eager to see again and spent way more money than I needed to. Oh and insurance doesn't cover the lenses, laser assisted surgery the surgical center or anesthesiologist, so out of pocket is several thousand dollars. Would I do it again? Just the cataract surgery without all the extras, yes.</text>< pictures>

< Review>
Was craving for some Thai food and decided to check this place out since it was close by. Came in around the afternoon and it wasn't packed; finding a seat was relatively easy. I ordered pad Thai and a curry. Pad Thai was flavorful, wet, and delicious. Really enjoyed it. The chicken curry was also really good, definitely a bit spicy but the flavors and aroma were exceptionally good. I really liked the decor as well, a large open space with wooden tables and seats. Overall, had a good time and enjoyed the food.<//Review>

<review>The 55 Thai Kitchen opened it's door to new customers less than a month ago. This locale - at1010 Broadway - is their third restaurant in the San Diego area ( There is one at SDSU at 5157 College Ave. and a second that is located in Golden Hill at 2601 Broadway. ).
I haven't eaten any Thai food lately however, whenever I've decided that I wanted to dine out at a Thai restaurant, I've always had several regular choices in mind : The new 55 Thai Kitchen is only a few blocks from my current apartment, so my choice was quite simple ; it's also across the street from Papa John's Pizza and Hodad,s Hamburger Place too.
Since I've never eaten any Thai dishes, served with curry - I'm much more familiar with foods from India, as they serve up many different curry dishes - I was surprised to learn that there are areas in Thailand that use quite a bit of curry, as a part of their dishes.
About two weeks ago, I talked to lady who had just dined there and she told me that their curry plates are very good! It wasn't until the 1st of June, that I received my check - I always try to save some money in order to dine out - so I decided to try 55 Thai Kitchen.
I ordered their " Curry" plate to go and it was awesome. My curry plate came with a generous helping of "healthy" brown rice and the curry itself contained slices of red and green peppers, potatoes and a very GENEROUS helping of both chicken and beef strips - the meats were exceptionally tender - in their spicy curry broth ( The plates come with a choice of chicken, beef or shrimp and it you want two meats, then it's $1 extra ).
I received quite a bit of help from their knowledgeable staff, as to the menu item that I had chosen and a good lesson in regards to Thailand and it's curry.
They have sixteen items on their menu, which includes appetizers, soup/salad, noodles and plates,as well as a variety of drinks too. Their prices are very reasonable and no plate is more than $9 in price.
The decor inside of their restaurant is quite beautiful; the tables are all made of polished wood, there are some nice plants and a skylight near the back, all creating a really neat dining atmosphere - a relaxing ambience/a good place for a few friends or else a small business get together.
I'm sure that all of their menu items are as good as both their "Yellow Curry" and "Green Curry" plates and I highly recommend that,  if you like any type of Asian foods, that you give them a try.
I tried 55 Thai Kitchen two more times over the 4th of July Holiday; one time I ordered my favourite, a yellow curry plate with chicken and beef and the second time I ordered shrimp, instead of beef.
I found that I now prefer to order indoors. My green curry plates had so much thinly sliced tender marinated white chicken breast in them, along with either beef or shrimp-the latter are only $1 extra-and with steamed carrots,squash and slices of red and green peppers, in a spicy flavoured broth; when I mixed my brown rice with everything, I had so much food that I could barely finish it.
While I was there, a large group of people came in and ordered and whatever they ordered, it sure looked good.
I just can't believe the amount of food you can get for only $9.70-inc.tax. The interior is simply beautiful, the music is great and I highly recommend that next time you'd like a really unique and cultural dining experience, that you give 55 Thai Kitchen a try.< /review>< rating>
5</rating>

<review>Andrea has gathered the best caliber of caring, knowledgeable, inspiring teachers overall of any studio I've known.  Frequent Iyengar and Alignment-based hatha offerings are the perfect complement to flow classes. In fact, I count on Iyengar's precise alignment and long pose-holding to make me stable and strong and keep me injury free in vinyasa classes. Iyengar is the basis of yoga and any serious student should not shortcut their practice without truly understanding the foundation of the asanas.I'm grateful for Satori and would recommend to all to get to know this sweet studio, conveniently located 1 block from Montgomery BART. <Name>Stefanie Jacinto Deo< /Name><UserId.>109749026645605660875<//UserId.><Rate>4</Rate><gmapID>0x80858062ff926673:0xb861c2c63f471f59</gmapID><Text>Great place to do yoga if you work in the financial district. My favorite teacher was Anne Barbaret. She does Iyengar Yoga which has a really strong focus on proper alignment, which was perfect for me as a beginner with some back issues. Anne was terrific about helping me modify some poses when I told her about my back concerns. I had wanted a class where I would have time to figure out how to do the pose correctly so as not to strain my lower back, as well as find my balance for the harder poses. The more fast-paced "flow" classes move pretty quickly from one pose to the next, so they were more challenging for me to keep up (and keep my balance).

For example, I took Hatha Flow yoga with Magi Khoo once and she was good. I worked up a nice sweat with some of the poses even though I wobbled through some of them. I took the same class with Allie Stark and she is a little more fast-paced than Magi. Even if the class is labeled as Level 1-3, Allie focuses on more advanced poses, like handstands, which was pretty intimidating for me. Allie seems to be a very popular teacher though because her classes are PACKED; if you arrive late, there is barely any floor space left for you.

I also took Monique Haan's Yin Yoga class once. There is a lot of meditation and it's definitely the slowest type of yoga, so it's great for de-stressing and easing into yoga after an injury, but not so much for working up a sweat.

There are several changing stalls and two very clean bathrooms. They also provide drinking water. Unfortunately there are no showers at this location. Satori Yoga is supposed to be moving to a new location soon on Sutter and Montgomery, and they've announced that they won't have showers there either.</Text>< pictures>

< review>
Rounding up from a 4.5.  It's in the back of the corner of a building structure, unassuming wing joint that is serving up a plethora of items from their menu.  Parking can be a bit of an issue though.

My favor I was the boneless wings in lemon and pepper sauce.  I will definitely be coming back for that.  My husband's chicken tenders were gigantic.  There's no rub or sauce on the chicken available for the tenders but you can get an order of sauce on the side.  The cheesy tots were great, we had a small order and we split it amongst the three of us.

My friend ordered wings, chicken fried rice, and onion rings.  He enjoyed himself immensely and was so happy to be there.

On Wednesday they have 75 cent wings.  I might have to try that out too.

There was plenty of food ordered and tons to take back home.  There's a lot of specials on the walls too.  The cashiers were helpful and the food came out promptly and hot!< /review>

< review>
Pros:
Friendly employees, tasty wings, rubs and sauces, able to order unbattered wings and decent prices.
Cons:
First off...I realize this is my problem but nutrition info is supposed to be available. No nutritional values available.  Descriptions are not sufficient to make a good decision on what to order.  I'm both diabetic and living a Keto lifestyle.   I need either better ingredient descriptions or complete nutrition facts in order to make an educated decision on what to order.
Second... no online ordering.
Lastly... sauced wings tend to be soggy
Overall: solid choice for wings in Westminster. You can get bigger wings at Wingstop but nowhere near the flavor.< /review>

<time>1477954221643< /time><Rate>3</Rate>< text>
There have been better occasions at this place.

Just ordering to go from socal wings and I'm a bit disappointed.  Their wet popcorn chicken was actually a bit dry. So unfortunate.

Also, they no longer offer free dipping sauces which is a complete bummer. You can buy the sauce for 50 cents each.

I'd stay away from the lychee lemonade. The small is crazily priced at $2.99. Also very disappointing. Too syrupy and sweet and thick. Just a confusing drink. The flavors don't really go together well in this drink.

Despite all the negative aspects, three stars bc the price and quantity is good. You get a lot of chicken in the small popcorn chicken for a reasonable 2.99. The flavors are good. I recommend mango madness. Finally, customer service is pretty nice, which is redeeming.</text>

< Review>
Obviously, as a GrubHub driver, I am privy to and receive a certain amount of respect and kindness shown to me by all restaurant employees. After all, we are colleagues and friends.

As for Red Robin in Roseville, California, I can tell you that a young lady named Kayla has shown me and our GrubHub customers a great deal of respect and kindness and assertiveness in making sure that each order is prepared correctly.

Believe me when I tell you that that is not where the service stops. Kindness and the art of loving and inclusiveness Has No Limitation.

So if you want to enjoy one America‚Äôs best burgers prepared in one of America‚Äôs best restaurants and served to you by one of the best servers in Roseville, California, go to Red Robin.

Ask for Kayla.

And let her present you with not just the best and most enjoyable night out, But one of the most heartfelt evenings you have ever experienced in your life.

I have to wonder how I could possibly be the kind of person that could know these beautiful human beings and call them friends.

And though I feel unworthy, you should present as if you are. Because You are...

Light and Love to You, dear friends.

Kayla, Sweetie darling, You are the bomb.</Review>

< text>
If you have food allergies this is the place to go for a really good restaurant burger. Their web site has a allergen menu where you check off what you cant eat and they give you options on what's on the menu you can have. Also shows ways you can have menu items by removing what your allergic to. I had the big taco tavern burger on a gluten free bun with no cheese or sliced peppers with a side salad. I usually get the steamed broccoli which is also bottomless. Love coming here, we've always had great service from the wait staff.< /text>

Catering Review:
I work for Toyota and I ordered the burger bar, salads, cookies, and other sides from Red Robins catering menu for our training event. We had lunch for 75 people 3 days in a row, all catered and delivered by Red Robin. We had a great experience each and every day from their team. The burger bar came with tons of fresh toppings and sauces, making it customizable and different each day. The salads were fresh, and cookies were a hit. The best part was that the Red Robin team was early each day, friendly, and stuck around to help set up the lunch for the event. We were more than thrilled with the food and service, and will definitely be using them again.</Text>

< review>
Ordered your onion rings for take out. The gal in the bar who helped was very nice. Gave me what I asked for. 4 pkgs. knife,fork,spoons./w salt & pepper. I wanted salt. I needed the salt. Got my order to the car. I was starving so had a ring. Oh my god. They looked alittle to dark but I was in the car & it was night. But when I took a bite, I thought my teeth would start breaking. They where so 'crunchy' , hard!. And yes , they where very dark. I remember the rings there golden brown /w a soft crunch & tender onion inside.not so done that you could'nt see it! Needless to say I went home & finished the 13 rings. ALOT of the crunch in the bottom of the box /w a small pool of grease. They where still warm to the very last one. How do they do that & still keep the crunch?  Anyway, I will give them another try some day, inside.. with a burger. I'll ask for medium oinon rings.< /review>
